Kubernetes RBAC authorization system is comprehensively implemented across multiple Go source files in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository. Here are the key components:\\n\\n## Core Authorization Engine\\n\\n**RBACAuthorizer** (plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/rbac.go) - The main authorizer implementing the authorizer.Authorizer interface. It contains the Authorize method that evaluates whether a request should be allowed based on RBAC rules. The authorizer uses a RequestToRuleMapper interface to resolve policy rules for users and namespaces. It implements a visitor pattern through authorizingVisitor to evaluate rules against request attributes.\\n\\n## Rule Resolution and Policy Evaluation\\n\\n**DefaultRuleResolver** (pkg/registry/rbac/validation/rule.go) - Implements comprehensive rule resolution for RBAC. It provides:\\n- RulesFor() method that accumulates all applicable policy rules for a user in a namespace\\n- VisitRulesFor() method that iterates through all applicable rules by visiting cluster-wide and namespace-scoped role bindings\\n- GetRoleReferenceRules() method that resolves Role or ClusterRole references from RoleBindings/ClusterRoleBindings\\n- Supports matching users against various subject types (Users, Groups, ServiceAccounts)\\n\\n## Subject Access Evaluation\\n\\n**SubjectAccessEvaluator** (plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/subject_locator.go) - Implements the SubjectLocator interface to determine which subjects are allowed to perform specific actions. The AllowedSubjects() method returns all subjects (users, groups, service accounts) that can perform a given action by examining applicable RoleBindings and ClusterRoleBindings.\\n\\n## REST API Handler\\n\\n**SubjectAccessReview REST Handler** (pkg/registry/authorization/subjectaccessreview/rest.go) - Handles SubjectAccessReview API requests. The REST struct with Create() method evaluates whether a user can perform an action and returns the decision status. It converts SubjectAccessReview specifications into authorization attributes and delegates to the authorizer for evaluation.\\n\\n## Bootstrap RBAC Policies\\n\\nBootstrap policy definitions are defined in plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/bootstrappolicy/:\\n- **policy.go** - Defines cluster-wide roles and role bindings including system roles (cluster-admin, system:nodes, etc.) and component roles (kube-controller-manager, kube-scheduler, etc.)\\n- **controller_policy.go** - Defines roles for Kubernetes controllers (replication controller manager, daemon set controller, etc.)\\n- **namespace_policy.go** - Defines namespace-scoped roles for system namespaces\\n\\nThese bootstrap policies are reconciled with the cluster in **pkg/registry/rbac/rest/storage_rbac.go** through the EnsureRBACPolicy() function which creates or updates bootstrap roles and role bindings.\\n\\n## Privilege Escalation Prevention\\n\\nPrivilege escalation is prevented through multiple policy-based storage implementations:\\n\\n**Role Storage** (pkg/registry/rbac/role/policybased/storage.go) - Wraps the standard storage for Roles with escalation checks. Create and Update methods verify that users cannot create/modify roles with permissions they don't already possess.\\n\\n**ClusterRole Storage** (pkg/registry/rbac/clusterrole/policybased/storage.go) - Similar escalation prevention for ClusterRoles with additional checks for aggregation rules which require cluster-admin privileges.\\n\\n**RoleBinding Storage** (pkg/registry/rbac/rolebinding/policybased/storage.go) - Prevents users from binding roles they're not authorized to use by verifying users have the \\\"bind\\\" privilege on the target role.\\n\\n**ClusterRoleBinding Storage** (pkg/registry/rbac/clusterrolebinding/policybased/storage.go) - Cluster-wide equivalent of role binding privilege escalation prevention.\\n\\n**Escalation Check Functions** (pkg/registry/rbac/escalation_check.go) - Provides utility functions:\\n- EscalationAllowed() - Checks if user is in system:masters group\\n- RoleEscalationAuthorized() - Verifies user has explicit \\\"escalate\\\" permission on roles\\n- BindingAuthorized() - Checks if user has \\\"bind\\\" permission for the referenced role\\n- ConfirmNoEscalation() - Core validation that ensures user doesn't grant permissions they don't possess\\n\\nThe escalation prevention is implemented by having the policy-based storage layers call ConfirmNoEscalation() through the AuthorizationRuleResolver, comparing rules the user is trying to create against the rules they currently possess, denying creation if it would escalate privileges.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3616,"cache_read_input_tokens":93663,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3616},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"e4180b14-9245-4603-b295-7f30daf86c68","uuid":"deb90cfb-768b-4dc6-b8f5-4d615069e1f9"}
